     {{cc
       {f 8192}
       {px x44862000
        {xc0600000 0}
        {x44600000 x43d70000}
        {x40600000 0}
        {xc0400000 xc1e00000}
        {x443a6000 x4418c000}
        {x40400000 x41e00000}
        {xc20a0000 xc0400000}
        {x44480000 x44256000}
        {x420a0000 x40400000}
        {xc1c00000 x42320000}
        {x44640000 x4416a000}
        {x41c00000 xc2320000}

        {xc2300000 xc1700000}}}     idem}
     {tx x44862000 x4457999a x4408d333}

  { selectAll str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 }

  { createEllipse str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 sb 1 }
  { createRectangle str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 sb 1 }
  { createRectangleCusped str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 sb 1 }
  { brush str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 sb 1 }
  { eraser src 2 str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 sb 1 }
  { clone src 1 str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 sb 1 }
  { reveal src 3 str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 sb 1 }
  { dodge src 1 str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 sb 1 }
  { burn src 1 str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 sb 1 }
  { blur src 1 str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 sb 1 }
  { sharpen src 1 str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 sb 1 }
  { smear src 1 str 1 ssx 1 ssy 1 sf 1 sb 1 }

Group {
 name LightSelectRebuild1
 tile_color 0x828b98ff
 xpos 41465
 ypos -4290
 addUserKnob {20 LightSelectRebuild}
 addUserKnob {22 Create l "Create Rebuild" t "Create an AOV Rebuild tree for all light select layers in the AOVs of the input pipe." T "import nuke\n\ndef unselect_all():\n    # Deselect all nodes\n    for n in nuke.allNodes(recurseGroups=True):\n        n.setSelected(False)\n\ndef make_node(nodeclass, pos_x, pos_y, nodeinput=None, nodename=None, knobvalues=''):\n    # Helper function to create a node with specified nodeclass, position, name and input\n    unselect_all()\n    node = nuke.createNode(nodeclass, knobvalues, inpanel=False)\n    node.setXYpos(pos_x, pos_y)\n    if nodeinput:\n        node.setInput(0, nodeinput)\n    if nodename:\n        node.setName(nodename)\n    nuke.autoplaceSnap(node)\n    return node\n\ndef get_layers(node, filters=None):\n    # Get all layers with a specified filter at the specified node\n    channels = node.channels()\n    layers = list(set(\[channel.split('.')\[0] for channel in channels]))\n    layers.sort()\n    # Keep only layers with filters if there is any\n    if filters:\n        new_layer_list = \[]\n        for layer in layers:\n            for filter_string in filters:\n                if filter_string.startswith('*'):\n                    # fuzzy search\n                    if filter_string\[1:] in layer:\n                        new_layer_list.append(layer)\n                elif filter_string.startswith('\$'):\n                    if layer.endswith(filter_string\[1:]):\n                        new_layer_list.append(layer)\n                else:\n                    if filter_string == layer:\n                        new_layer_list.append(layer)\n        layers = new_layer_list\n    return layers\n\n\n\ndef ls_create(lslayer, lsnum, specnum, diffnum, base_dot, base_ls_replace, spec=False):\n    # Create one tree for a light select layer. Can be LGT (default) or Specular (if spec=True)\n    print \"Setting up\", lslayer, \"number:\", lsnum\n\n    # Start 4 grid spaces to the right\n    if spec:\n        xpos = (base_dot.xpos()) - grid_x * 2\n    else:\n        xpos = (base_dot.xpos()) - grid_x * 4\n    \n    ypos = base_dot.ypos()\n\n    base_dot = make_node('Dot', xpos, ypos, base_dot, '\{0\}_start_diffuse_dot'.format(lslayer))\n\n    ls_shuffle = make_node('Shuffle', xpos, ypos+grid_y*4, nodeinput=base_dot, knobvalues='in \{0\} label \\\[value\\ in\\]'.format(lslayer))\n    \n    # Base Light Select AOV\n    base_ls_dot = make_node('Dot', xpos, ls_shuffle.ypos()+grid_y*3, nodeinput=ls_shuffle, knobvalues='label \{0\}'.format(lslayer), nodename='\{0\}_start_dot'.format(lslayer))\n\n    ls_grade = make_node('Multiply', xpos, base_ls_dot.ypos()+grid_y*6, nodeinput=base_ls_dot, nodename='Mult_\{0\}'.format(lslayer))\n    ls_grade.addKnob(nuke.Color_Knob('exposure', ''))\n    ls_grade\['exposure'].setRange(-10,10)\n    ls_grade\['exposure'].setSingleValue(True)\n    ls_grade\['value'].setExpression('pow(2, exposure)')\n    ls_grade\['value'].setSingleValue(False)\n\n    ls_end_dot = make_node('Dot', xpos, ls_grade.ypos()+grid_y*22, nodeinput=ls_grade, nodename='\{0\}_end_dot'.format(lslayer))\n    if spec:\n      ls_end_dot.setXYpos(ls_end_dot.xpos(), ls_end_dot.ypos() + grid_y*2)\n\n\n    # Connect this light select layer to the proper merge nodes\n    if spec:\n        if specnum >= 2:\n            # Don't connect the mask input\n            specnum += 1\n        spec_merge_orig = nuke.toNode('_LS_SPEC_ORIG_')\n        spec_merge_out = nuke.toNode('_LS_SPEC_OUT_')\n        spec_merge_orig.setInput(specnum, base_ls_dot)\n        spec_merge_out.setInput(specnum, ls_end_dot)\n\n        # Hacky: assumes diff of same name came before\n        diff_mult_node_name = \"Mult_\" + lslayer\[:-5] + \"_diff\"\n        print diff_mult_node_name\n        diff_mult_node = nuke.toNode(diff_mult_node_name)\n        diff_mult_node\['value'].setExpression('parent.\{0\}.value'.format(ls_grade.name()))\n\n    else:\n        if diffnum >= 2:\n            # Don't connect the mask input\n            diffnum += 1\n        diff_merge_orig = nuke.toNode('_LS_DIFF_ORIG_')\n        diff_merge_out = nuke.toNode('_LS_DIFF_OUT_')\n        diff_merge_orig.setInput(diffnum, base_ls_dot)\n        diff_merge_out.setInput(diffnum, ls_end_dot)\n\n\n    # Replace lightselect AOV\n    lsreplace_dot = make_node('Dot', base_ls_replace.xpos()-grid_x, base_ls_replace.ypos()+grid_y*2, nodeinput=ls_end_dot)\n    lsreplace_dot\['hide_input'].setValue(True)\n    # lsreplace_premult = make_node('Premult', base_ls_replace.xpos()-grid_x, lsreplace_dot.ypos()+grid_y, nodeinput=lsreplace_dot)\n    lsreplace_shufflecopy = make_node('ShuffleCopy', base_ls_replace.xpos(), base_ls_replace.ypos()+grid_y*2, nodeinput=base_ls_replace, nodename='LSReplace_\{0\}'.format(lslayer), knobvalues='red red green green blue blue alpha alpha out \{0\}'.format(lslayer))\n    lsreplace_shufflecopy.setInput(1, lsreplace_dot)\n\n\n    # Connect output to last lsreplace shufflecopy\n    nuke.toNode('_FINAL_PREMULT_').setInput(0, lsreplace_shufflecopy)\n\n    base_ls_replace = lsreplace_shufflecopy\n\n    return base_dot, base_ls_replace\n\n\n\n# Create Light Select AOV Breakouts\n# grid_x = int(nuke.toNode('preferences').knob('GridWidth').value())\n# grid_y = int(nuke.toNode('preferences').knob('GridHeight').value())\ngrid_x = 134\ngrid_y = 40\n\nnode = nuke.thisNode()\n\nnuke.root().begin()\nlslayers = get_layers(node, filters=\[\"\$_diff\", \"\$_spec\"])\n\nnode.begin()\n\nbase_dot = nuke.toNode('_INPUT_AOVS_START_')\nbase_ls_replace = nuke.toNode('_LS_REPLACE_AOVS_')\n\n# print \"Starting with:\", base_dot.name()\nprint \"LAYERS:\\n\", '\\n'.join(lslayers)\n\nspecnum = 0\ndiffnum = 0\nfor i, lslayer in enumerate(lslayers):\n    # Determine if lightselect is direct specular or diffuse\n    if lslayer.endswith(\"_spec\"):\n        spec = True\n    if lslayer.endswith(\"_diff\"):\n        spec = False\n\n    base_dot, base_ls_replace = ls_create(lslayer, i, specnum, diffnum, base_dot, base_ls_replace, spec)\n\n    if spec:\n        specnum += 1\n    else: \n        diffnum += 1\n\n    if node\['create_controller_knobs'].getValue():\n        # Add Tab for Light Select if diff (sloppy, assumes there are diff/spec pairs)\n        # if \"_diff\" in lslayer:\n        #     node.addKnob(nuke.Tab_Knob('_'.join(lslayer.split('_')\[0:-1])))\n        \n        # Only add spec controls (will be expression linked internally)\n        if \"_spec\" in lslayer:\n            # Add label for the grade knobs on this lightselect\n            label_knob = nuke.Text_Knob('divider_label_'+lslayer)\n            label_knob.setValue(\" \")\n            label_knob.setLabel(\"@b;\"+lslayer.split('_spec')\[0])\n            node.addKnob(label_knob)\n            \n            # Add linked knobs to grade for this lightselect\n            # Link_Knobs are weird and hard to retrieve the Link_Knob knob object instead of the referent\n            # http://community.thefoundry.co.uk/discussion/topic.aspx?f=190&t=102091\n            # You have to use node.allKnobs() and the get Link_Knob objects. Or node.knobs()\['knobname']\n\n            lsgrade = nuke.toNode('Mult_\{0\}'.format(lslayer))\n            # lsgrade_knobs = \['black', 'white', 'multiply', 'add', 'gamma']\n            lsgrade_knobs = \['exposure']\n\n            for knob in lsgrade_knobs:\n                knoblink = nuke.Link_Knob(knob+\"_Link_Knob_\"+lslayer)\n                knoblink.makeLink(lsgrade.name(), knob)\n                knoblink.setLabel('exposure')\n                node.addKnob(knoblink)\nnuke.root().begin()\n# Copy to nodegraph automatically if the auto_copy_to_nodegraph is checked, then self destruct\nif node\['auto_copy_to_nodegraph'].getValue():\n    node\['CopyToNodegraph'].execute()\n    unselect_all()\n    node.setSelected(True)\n    nuke.delete(node)" +STARTLINE}
 addUserKnob {26 spacer l " &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;" -STARTLINE T " "}
 addUserKnob {22 CopyToNodegraph l "Copy To Nodegraph" t "Copy the AOV Rebuild tree into the node graph." -STARTLINE T "## Copy LightSelectRebuild graph to node graph\nnode = nuke.thisNode()\n\nnuke.root().begin()\nnode.begin()\n\[n.setSelected(True) for n in nuke.allNodes() if \"Input\" not in n.name() and \"Output\" not in n.name()]\nnuke.nodeCopy(\"%clipboard%\")\nnuke.root().begin()\nnuke.nodePaste(\"%clipboard%\")"}

Group {
 name LightSelectRebuild
 tile_color 0x828b98ff
 xpos 39948
 ypos -4229
 addUserKnob {20 LightSelectRebuild}
 addUserKnob {22 Create l "Create Rebuild" t "Create an AOV Rebuild tree for all light select layers in the AOVs of the input pipe." T "import nuke\n\ndef unselect_all():\n    # Deselect all nodes\n    for n in nuke.allNodes(recurseGroups=True):\n        n.setSelected(False)\n\ndef make_node(nodeclass, pos_x, pos_y, nodeinput=None, nodename=None, knobvalues=''):\n    # Helper function to create a node with specified nodeclass, position, name and input\n    unselect_all()\n    node = nuke.createNode(nodeclass, knobvalues, inpanel=False)\n    node.setXYpos(pos_x, pos_y)\n    if nodeinput:\n        node.setInput(0, nodeinput)\n    if nodename:\n        node.setName(nodename)\n    nuke.autoplaceSnap(node)\n    return node\n\ndef get_layers(node, filters=None):\n    # Get all layers with a specified filter at the specified node\n    channels = node.channels()\n    layers = list(set(\[channel.split('.')\[0] for channel in channels]))\n    layers.sort()\n    # Keep only layers with filters if there is any\n    if filters:\n        new_layer_list = \[]\n        for layer in layers:\n            for filter_string in filters:\n                if filter_string.startswith('*'):\n                    # fuzzy search\n                    if filter_string\[1:] in layer:\n                        new_layer_list.append(layer)\n                elif filter_string.startswith('\$'):\n                    if layer.endswith(filter_string\[1:]):\n                        new_layer_list.append(layer)\n                else:\n                    if filter_string == layer:\n                        new_layer_list.append(layer)\n        layers = new_layer_list\n    return layers\n\n\n\ndef ls_create(lslayer, lsnum, specnum, diffnum, base_dot, base_ls_replace, spec=False):\n    # Create one tree for a light select layer. Can be LGT (default) or Specular (if spec=True)\n    print \"Setting up\", lslayer, \"number:\", lsnum\n\n    # Start 4 grid spaces to the right\n    if spec:\n        xpos = (base_dot.xpos()) - grid_x * 2\n    else:\n        xpos = (base_dot.xpos()) - grid_x * 4\n    \n    ypos = base_dot.ypos()\n\n    base_dot = make_node('Dot', xpos, ypos, base_dot, '\{0\}_start_diffuse_dot'.format(lslayer))\n\n    ls_shuffle = make_node('Shuffle', xpos, ypos+grid_y*4, nodeinput=base_dot, knobvalues='in \{0\} label \\\[value\\ in\\]'.format(lslayer))\n    \n    # Base Light Select AOV\n    base_ls_dot = make_node('Dot', xpos, ls_shuffle.ypos()+grid_y*3, nodeinput=ls_shuffle, knobvalues='label \{0\}'.format(lslayer), nodename='\{0\}_start_dot'.format(lslayer))\n\n    ls_grade = make_node('Multiply', xpos, base_ls_dot.ypos()+grid_y*6, nodeinput=base_ls_dot, nodename='Mult_\{0\}'.format(lslayer))\n    ls_grade.addKnob(nuke.Color_Knob('exposure', ''))\n    ls_grade\['exposure'].setRange(-10,10)\n    ls_grade\['exposure'].setSingleValue(True)\n    ls_grade\['value'].setExpression('pow(2, exposure)')\n    ls_grade\['value'].setSingleValue(False)\n\n    ls_end_dot = make_node('Dot', xpos, ls_grade.ypos()+grid_y*22, nodeinput=ls_grade, nodename='\{0\}_end_dot'.format(lslayer))\n    if spec:\n      ls_end_dot.setXYpos(ls_end_dot.xpos(), ls_end_dot.ypos() + grid_y*2)\n\n\n    # Connect this light select layer to the proper merge nodes\n    if spec:\n        if specnum >= 2:\n            # Don't connect the mask input\n            specnum += 1\n        spec_merge_orig = nuke.toNode('_LS_SPEC_ORIG_')\n        spec_merge_out = nuke.toNode('_LS_SPEC_OUT_')\n        spec_merge_orig.setInput(specnum, base_ls_dot)\n        spec_merge_out.setInput(specnum, ls_end_dot)\n\n        # Hacky: assumes diff of same name came before\n        diff_mult_node_name = \"Mult_\" + lslayer\[:-5] + \"_diff\"\n        print diff_mult_node_name\n        diff_mult_node = nuke.toNode(diff_mult_node_name)\n        diff_mult_node\['value'].setExpression('parent.\{0\}.value'.format(ls_grade.name()))\n\n    else:\n        if diffnum >= 2:\n            # Don't connect the mask input\n            diffnum += 1\n        diff_merge_orig = nuke.toNode('_LS_DIFF_ORIG_')\n        diff_merge_out = nuke.toNode('_LS_DIFF_OUT_')\n        diff_merge_orig.setInput(diffnum, base_ls_dot)\n        diff_merge_out.setInput(diffnum, ls_end_dot)\n\n\n    # Replace lightselect AOV\n    lsreplace_dot = make_node('Dot', base_ls_replace.xpos()-grid_x, base_ls_replace.ypos()+grid_y*2, nodeinput=ls_end_dot)\n    lsreplace_dot\['hide_input'].setValue(True)\n    # lsreplace_premult = make_node('Premult', base_ls_replace.xpos()-grid_x, lsreplace_dot.ypos()+grid_y, nodeinput=lsreplace_dot)\n    lsreplace_shufflecopy = make_node('ShuffleCopy', base_ls_replace.xpos(), base_ls_replace.ypos()+grid_y*2, nodeinput=base_ls_replace, nodename='LSReplace_\{0\}'.format(lslayer), knobvalues='red red green green blue blue alpha alpha out \{0\}'.format(lslayer))\n    lsreplace_shufflecopy.setInput(1, lsreplace_dot)\n\n\n    # Connect output to last lsreplace shufflecopy\n    nuke.toNode('_FINAL_PREMULT_').setInput(0, lsreplace_shufflecopy)\n\n    base_ls_replace = lsreplace_shufflecopy\n\n    return base_dot, base_ls_replace\n\n\n\n# Create Light Select AOV Breakouts\n# grid_x = int(nuke.toNode('preferences').knob('GridWidth').value())\n# grid_y = int(nuke.toNode('preferences').knob('GridHeight').value())\ngrid_x = 134\ngrid_y = 40\n\nnode = nuke.thisNode()\n\nnuke.root().begin()\nlslayers = get_layers(node, filters=\[\"\$_diff\", \"\$_spec\"])\n\nnode.begin()\n\nbase_dot = nuke.toNode('_INPUT_AOVS_START_')\nbase_ls_replace = nuke.toNode('_LS_REPLACE_AOVS_')\n\n# print \"Starting with:\", base_dot.name()\nprint \"LAYERS:\\n\", '\\n'.join(lslayers)\n\nspecnum = 0\ndiffnum = 0\nfor i, lslayer in enumerate(lslayers):\n    # Determine if lightselect is direct specular or diffuse\n    if lslayer.endswith(\"_spec\"):\n        spec = True\n    if lslayer.endswith(\"_diff\"):\n        spec = False\n\n    base_dot, base_ls_replace = ls_create(lslayer, i, specnum, diffnum, base_dot, base_ls_replace, spec)\n\n    if spec:\n        specnum += 1\n    else: \n        diffnum += 1\n\n    if node\['create_controller_knobs'].getValue():\n        # Add Tab for Light Select if diff (sloppy, assumes there are diff/spec pairs)\n        # if \"_diff\" in lslayer:\n        #     node.addKnob(nuke.Tab_Knob('_'.join(lslayer.split('_')\[0:-1])))\n        \n        # Only add spec controls (will be expression linked internally)\n        if \"_spec\" in lslayer:\n            # Add label for the grade knobs on this lightselect\n            label_knob = nuke.Text_Knob('divider_label_'+lslayer)\n            label_knob.setValue(\" \")\n            label_knob.setLabel(\"@b;\"+lslayer.split('_spec')\[0])\n            node.addKnob(label_knob)\n            \n            # Add linked knobs to grade for this lightselect\n            # Link_Knobs are weird and hard to retrieve the Link_Knob knob object instead of the referent\n            # http://community.thefoundry.co.uk/discussion/topic.aspx?f=190&t=102091\n            # You have to use node.allKnobs() and the get Link_Knob objects. Or node.knobs()\['knobname']\n\n            lsgrade = nuke.toNode('Mult_\{0\}'.format(lslayer))\n            # lsgrade_knobs = \['black', 'white', 'multiply', 'add', 'gamma']\n            lsgrade_knobs = \['exposure']\n\n            for knob in lsgrade_knobs:\n                knoblink = nuke.Link_Knob(knob+\"_Link_Knob_\"+lslayer)\n                knoblink.makeLink(lsgrade.name(), knob)\n                knoblink.setLabel('exposure')\n                node.addKnob(knoblink)\nnuke.root().begin()\n# Copy to nodegraph automatically if the auto_copy_to_nodegraph is checked, then self destruct\nif node\['auto_copy_to_nodegraph'].getValue():\n    node\['CopyToNodegraph'].execute()\n    unselect_all()\n    node.setSelected(True)\n    nuke.delete(node)" +STARTLINE}
